<h3>Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>External gateway supervision:</strong> add <code>OPENCLAW_SUPERVISOR_MODE=external</code> for lifecycle owners such as OCM, preserving verified restart and deferral behavior without exposing native service authority, blocking native service mutation and self-update, and providing a versioned atomic restart-handoff consume contract. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a>.</li>
<li><strong>ClickClack guided setup:</strong> configure ClickClack from <code>openclaw onboard</code> or <code>openclaw channels add clickclack</code> with URL, token, and workspace prompts, default-account env fallback, nonfatal live connection validation, and gateway-aware next steps that connect automatically when OpenClaw is already running. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a>.</li>
<li><strong>ClickClack command menus:</strong> publish each bot's native OpenClaw commands to ClickClack composer autocomplete at gateway startup, with per-account opt-out and nonfatal compatibility handling for older tokens and servers. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a> and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Skill Workshop approvals:</strong> run agent-initiated apply, reject, and quarantine actions without an additional approval prompt by default while preserving <code>skills.workshop.approvalPolicy: "pending"</code> as an opt-in approval gate. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a>.</li>
<li><strong>TUI fuzzy selectors:</strong> delegate list matching to pi-tui, adding slash-token and alpha-number matching while removing the local matcher fork.</li>
<li><strong>macOS paired-node terminals:</strong> advertise duplex Codex and Claude terminal resume commands from the embedded node host and forward interactive input and cancellation through the native app bridge. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4881711349" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/107335" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/issues/107335/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/107335">#107335</a>)</li>
<li><strong>Control UI catalog terminals:</strong> open eligible Codex and Claude Code sessions in the native CLI on their Gateway or paired-node host, with viewer-versus-terminal preferences, validated resume commands, and an interactive PTY relay. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4879680703" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/107086" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/107086/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/107086">#107086</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Skill Workshop history review:</strong> add a manual, newest-first session scan that progressively searches older substantial work for conservative skill ideas, stores only SQLite cursor metadata, and leaves up to three results as pending proposals even when autonomous self-learning is disabled. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4871736231" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/106182" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/issues/106182/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/106182">#106182</a>)</li>

<h3>Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>External gateway supervision:</strong> add <code>OPENCLAW_SUPERVISOR_MODE=external</code> for lifecycle owners such as OCM, preserving verified restart and deferral behavior without exposing native service authority, blocking native service mutation and self-update, and providing a versioned atomic restart-handoff consume contract. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a>.</li>
<li><strong>ClickClack guided setup:</strong> configure ClickClack from <code>openclaw onboard</code> or <code>openclaw channels add clickclack</code> with URL, token, and workspace prompts, default-account env fallback, nonfatal live connection validation, and gateway-aware next steps that connect automatically when OpenClaw is already running. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a>.</li>
<li><strong>ClickClack command menus:</strong> publish each bot's native OpenClaw commands to ClickClack composer autocomplete at gateway startup, with per-account opt-out and nonfatal compatibility handling for older tokens and servers. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a> and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Skill Workshop approvals:</strong> run agent-initiated apply, reject, and quarantine actions without an additional approval prompt by default while preserving <code>skills.workshop.approvalPolicy: "pending"</code> as an opt-in approval gate. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a>.</li>
<li><strong>TUI fuzzy selectors:</strong> delegate list matching to pi-tui, adding slash-token and alpha-number matching while removing the local matcher fork.</li>
<li><strong>macOS paired-node terminals:</strong> advertise duplex Codex and Claude terminal resume commands from the embedded node host and forward interactive input and cancellation through the native app bridge. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4881711349" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/107335" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/issues/107335/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/107335">#107335</a>)</li>
<li><strong>Control UI catalog terminals:</strong> open eligible Codex and Claude Code sessions in the native CLI on their Gateway or paired-node host, with viewer-versus-terminal preferences, validated resume commands, and an interactive PTY relay. <h3>Fixes</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>Cloud worker derived workspace caches:</strong> exclude Python caches, dependency trees, and macOS metadata symmetrically from outbound sync and inbound reconciliation so local cache rewrites cannot fence later cloud results or worker reclaim.</li>
<li><strong>Codex model status diagnostics:</strong> report a configured Codex route as unavailable when its harness plugin is disabled, missing, or quarantined, while preserving the separate credential result and making <code>models status --check</code> fail instead of silently treating fallback execution as healthy. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Gateway control-plane rate limiting:</strong> use per-method buckets with a 30-per-minute budget so interactive admin writes remain responsive while retaining runaway-loop protection.</li>
<li><strong>Signal shutdown delivery:</strong> drain already-accepted ingress before stopping the monitor so messages received immediately before shutdown finish processing instead of being dropped.</li>
<li><strong>External supervisor restart health:</strong> accept device-identity policy closes only when the replacement gateway lock and listener PID agree, preventing OCM-managed restarts from timing out after a successful handoff. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/shakkernerd/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/shakkernerd">@shakkernerd</a>.</li>
<li><strong>ACPX cleanup process inspection:</strong> bound host process-table reads so stalled <code>ps</code> calls cannot hang gateway startup or session cleanup while retaining fail-closed ownership checks. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/Alix-007/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/Alix-007">@Alix-007</a>.</li>
